## Release 0.9.202507150 (2025-12-23 09-47-21 UTC)

#### Notes
* update to rolling release 2025-07-15T12:32:10Z
* remove obsolete firewall zone plan adjustment handling code

* implement manual firewall zone overrides and plan adjustments
* add firewall zone plan adjustment handling for create and update operations

## Release 0.7.202507150 (2025-12-23 04-29-06 UTC)
### Project changes
#### Bug fixes
* inline firewall zone `from` bindings so OpenTofu can push zone membership and cross-zone rules in a single transaction, preventing transient lockouts when applying firewall changes

#### Bug fixes
* improve log masking for API key and endpoint to prevent crashes with special characters
* enhance delete operations for state attributes not in plan, including nested attributes
* pass client pointer to resetListValueIfNeeded for correct staged delete operations
* improve list attribute reset logic in resetListValueIfNeeded function
* enhance list attribute deletion logic in resetListValueIfNeeded function
* simplify list attribute reset logic in resetListValueIfNeeded function
* enhance list attribute handling in resetListValueIfNeeded function
* improve handling of list-like attributes in update logic
* add live state refresh before update to prevent configuration drift
* improve list value reset logic to avoid unnecessary deletions and handle ordering differences
* enhance update logic to handle list value resets and improve state management
* changelog generation nil dereference error
* merged conntrack-sync resources
* merge dhcp-server subnet range
* remove redundant makefile dependency and debug prints
* nil pointer error during some change types
* removed dhcp-server subnet merge
* remove child nodes from schema and resource model where they should not be
* unconfigured lists caused panic
* allows for IP addresses to be used in named resource identifiers as described in #222
* generate go from xsd with installed tooling instead of imported tooling
* skip bugged release
* minor versioning reset bug and changelog typeos
* multivalue elements dereferencing during vyos api data generation
* changelog error on non conventional commit message
* remove tfsdk tags for child-exists parameters
* handle unknown attributes
* reduce retry count to avoid excessive timeouts
* temporary directory creation
* tenv autoinstall
* fix makefile erroring out on file deletion
* doc generation with opensource tooling
* resource identifier attribute
* Makefile shell substitution and git cmd error
* remove redundant and error prone pre-commit run
* base changelog generation on previous tag instead of previous commit
* fixed error in versioning
* changelog and release procedures
* generate files with relative path in autogen comment
* move autogen comment to use relative path to avoid changes between machines
* makefile improvements and CI fixes
* auto update github action
* add missing manifest required by goreleaser
* removed unintended increase in fix version
* Improve publishing target
* publish packaging zips and docs
* fix release process
* fixed vyosOps gen mangling bug
* GenerateVyosOps() some times returns a mangled result, reason unknown. Attempt to fix the issue
* half working when resource is empty
* resource parent IDs now work and are documented as numbers when they should be
* concurrent requests getting muddled
* vyos interface definition update method
* removed redundant ignore flag and added initial helper function for resource child detection
* Several (un-)marshaling and api client errors
* Added id field to reasources
* Vyos interfaces that has breaking line changes, also keep quotes for strings

* nil pointer error during some change types
* removed dhcp-server subnet merge
* remove child nodes from schema and resource model where they should not be
* unconfigured lists caused panic
* allows for IP addresses to be used in named resource identifiers as described in #222
* generate go from xsd with installed tooling instead of imported tooling
* skip bugged release
* minor versioning reset bug and changelog typeos
* multivalue elements dereferencing during vyos api data generation
* changelog error on non conventional commit message
* remove tfsdk tags for child-exists parameters
* handle unknown attributes
* reduce retry count to avoid excessive timeouts
* temporary directory creation
* tenv autoinstall
* fix makefile erroring out on file deletion
* doc generation with opensource tooling
* resource identifier attribute
* Makefile shell substitution and git cmd error
* remove redundant and error prone pre-commit run
* base changelog generation on previous tag instead of previous commit
* fixed error in versioning
* changelog and release procedures
* generate files with relative path in autogen comment
* move autogen comment to use relative path to avoid changes between machines
* makefile improvements and CI fixes
* auto update github action
* add missing manifest required by goreleaser
* removed unintended increase in fix version
* Improve publishing target
* publish packaging zips and docs
* fix release process
* fixed vyosOps gen mangling bug
* GenerateVyosOps() some times returns a mangled result, reason unknown. Attempt to fix the issue
* half working when resource is empty
* resource parent IDs now work and are documented as numbers when they should be
* concurrent requests getting muddled
* vyos interface definition update method
* removed redundant ignore flag and added initial helper function for resource child detection
* Several (un-)marshaling and api client errors
* Added id field to reasources
* Vyos interfaces that has breaking line changes, also keep quotes for strings
